SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 14:56:11') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 14:56:12') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 14:56:26') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:22:49') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:27:00') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:27:00') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:41:10') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:41:11') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:41:17') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:41:22') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:41:22') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC

SELECT a.id, a.name, a.alias, a.image, a.quantity, a.price, b.product_id, b.promotion_id, b.quantity AS discount_quantity, b.quantity_user, b.sold AS discount_sold, b.price AS discount_price, b.percent, b.`type`, b.date_end, b.date_start 
                FROM fs_products AS a INNER JOIN fs_promotion_discount_detail AS b ON a.id = b.product_id 
                WHERE b.published = 1 AND a.published = 1 AND a.price > 0 AND DATE(b.date_end) >= DATE('2024-07-11 16:41:22') AND ((b.quantity > 0 AND b.sold < b.quantity) OR (b.quantity = 0))
                ORDER BY a.ordering DESC, a.id DESC
